{"id":"FRG-246","title":"Objects change sprite when state transitions","description":"## Problem

The stove stays as stove_off.png even when its state is cooking or done. Books stay closed. Easel stays blank. Object state machines work internally but have no visual feedback.

## Available Assets

* stove_off.png / stove_on.png
* book_closed.png / book_open.png
* easel_blank.png / easel_painting.png / easel_finished.png
* cup_empty.png / cup_full.png

## What to do

1. Define a sprite map per object: { stateName: spriteKey }
2. On each state transition (in objectEngine), emit the new sprite key
3. Scene.js swaps the sprite texture on the Phaser game object
4. Map: stove cooking/done->stove_on, idle->stove_off; bookshelf reading->book_open, idle->book_closed; easel painting->easel_painting, done->easel_finished, idle->easel_blank; tea_set brewing/ready->cup_full, idle->cup_empty

USERMESSAGE #15
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * objects.js — interactive object state machines for the Japanese Home scene.
     3→ *
     4→ * Each object definition has:
     5→ *   { id, name, position: { tx, ty }, interactMs, state, states }
     6→ *
     7→ * Each state can have:
     8→ *   transitions: { use: { next: 'stateName' } }   — triggered by interact()
     9→ *   auto_next:   { state: 'stateName', after: N }  — fires automatically after N seconds
    10→ *   speech:      'string'                           — shown as character speech bubble
    11→ *   emoji:       '🍳'                               — floating emoji on transition
    12→ */
    13→
    14→// ── Object definitions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    15→// Japanese Home (912×642, 19×13 tiles, 48px each).
    16→// Walkable interior: cols 1–17, rows 2–9.
    17→
    18→export const OBJECT_DEFS = [
    19→  {
    20→    id: 'stove',
    21→    name: 'stove',
    22→    capacity: 1,
    23→    interactAnim: 'phone',
    24→    position: { tx: 3, ty: 3 },
    25→    interactMs: 8000,
    26→    state: 'idle',
    27→    states: {
    28→      idle: {
    29→        transitions: { use: { next: 'cooking' } },
    30→      },
    31→      cooking: {
    32→        speech: 'Let me cook something...',
    33→        auto_next: { state: 'done', after: 30 },
    34→      },
    35→      done: {
    36→        emoji: '🍳',
    37→        speech: "Dinner's ready! 🍳",
    38→        auto_next: { state: 'idle', after: 60 },
    39→        transitions: { use: { next: 'idle' } },
    40→      },
    41→    },
    42→  },
    43→  {
    44→    id: 'fridge',
    45→    name: 'fridge',
    46→    capacity: 1,
    47→    interactAnim: 'phone',
    48→    position: { tx: 2, ty: 3 },
    49→    interactMs: 5000,
    50→    state: 'idle',
    51→    states: {
    52→      idle: {
    53→        transitions: { use: { next: 'open' } },

   224→];
   225→
   226→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   227→
   228→class ObjectInstance {
   229→  constructor(def) {
   230→    this.id          = def.id;
   231→    this.name        = def.name;
   232→    this.label       = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   233→    this.position    = def.position;
   234→    this.tx          = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   235→    this.ty          = def.position.ty;
   236→    this.states      = def.states;
   237→    this.state       = def.state || 'idle';
   238→    this.interactAnim = def.interactAnim || null;
   239→    this.interactMs  = def.interactMs || 8000;
   240→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   241→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   242→
   243→    // Slot system
   244→    this.capacity      = def.capacity ?? 1;
   245→    this._reservations = new Set(); // charNames walking toward this object
   246→    this._occupants    = new Set(); // charNames actively interacting
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  /** True if no more slots are available (reserved + occupied >= capacity). */
   250→  isFull() {
   251→    return this._reservations.size + this._occupants.size >= this.capacity;
   252→  }
   253→
   254→  /**
   255→   * Reserve a slot for charName before they start walking.
   256→   * Returns true if the reservation succeeded, false if the object is full.
   257→   */
   258→  reserve(charName) {
   259→    if (this.isFull()) return false;
   260→    this._reservations.add(charName);
   261→    return true;
   262→  }
   263→
   264→  /**
   265→   * Called when charName arrives at the object.
   266→   * Converts the reservation to an active occupancy.
   267→   */
   268→  arrive(charName) {
   269→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   270→    this._occupants.add(charName);
   271→  }
   272→
   273→  /**
   274→   * Release a slot when the character finishes interacting or abandons the walk.
   275→   * Warns if charName was not a known occupant or reservation — signals an orphaned slot.
   276→   */
   277→  release(charName) {
   278→    if (!this._reservations.has(charName) && !this._occupants.has(charName)) {
   279→      console.warn(
   280→        `[objects] release('${this.id}', '${charName}'): ` +
   281→        `not a known occupant or reservation — possible orphaned slot`
   282→      );
   283→    }
   284→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   285→    this._occupants.delete(charName);
   286→  }
   287→
   288→  /** Returns the names of characters who have reserved a slot (walking toward this object). */
   289→  getReservations() { return Array.from(this._reservations); }
   290→
   291→  /** Returns the names of characters who are actively occupying a slot. */
   292→  getOccupants() { return Array.from(this._occupants); }
   293→
   294→  /** Clear all reservations and occupancies (used on sim reset). */
   295→  clearSlots() {
   296→    this._reservations.clear();
   297→    this._occupants.clear();
   298→  }
   299→
   300→  /**
   301→   * Returns current slot occupancy info.
   302→   * @returns {{ capacity, reserved, occupied, available }}
   303→   */
   304→  getSlotInfo() {
   305→    return {
   306→      capacity:  this.capacity,
   307→      reserved:  this._reservations.size,
   308→      occupied:  this._occupants.size,
   309→      available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size,
   310→    };
   311→  }
   312→
   313→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   314→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   315→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   316→  }
   317→
   318→  /**
   319→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   320→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   321→   */
   322→  interact(action = 'use') {
   323→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   324→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   325→    if (!tr) return null;
   326→
   327→    this.state = tr.next;
   328→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   329→
   330→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   331→    return {
   332→      objectId: this.id,
   333→      state:    this.state,
   334→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   335→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   336→    };
   337→  }
   338→
   339→  /**
   340→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   341→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   342→   */
   343→  tick(deltaMs) {
   344→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   345→
   346→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   347→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   348→
   349→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   350→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   351→
   352→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   353→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   354→
   355→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   356→    return {
   357→      objectId: this.id,
   358→      state:    this.state,
   359→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   360→      auto:     true,
   361→    };
   362→  }
   363→}
   364→
   365→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   366→
   367→export class ObjectEngine {
   368→  constructor() {
   369→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   370→  }
   371→
   372→  addObjects(defs) {
   373→    for (const def of defs) {
   374→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   375→    }
   376→  }
   377→
   378→  /**
   379→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   380→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   381→   */
   382→  tick(deltaMs) {
   383→    const events = [];
   384→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   385→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   386→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   387→    }
   388→    return events;
   389→  }
   390→
   391→  /**
   392→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   393→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   394→   */
   395→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   396→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   397→  }
   398→
   399→  getAll()    { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   400→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   401→
   402→  reserve(objectId, charName) { return this._map.get(objectId)?.reserve(charName) ?? false; }
   403→  arrive(objectId, charName)  { this._map.get(objectId)?.arrive(charName); }
   404→  release(objectId, charName) { this._map.get(objectId)?.release(charName); }
   405→  clearSlots(objectId)        { this._map.get(objectId)?.clearSlots(); }
   406→  clearAllSlots()             { for (const obj of this._map.values()) obj.clearSlots(); }
   407→}

    47→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    48→  const grid = [];
    49→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {

    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}

    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        buildDynamicWalkable: (char) => this._buildDynamicWalkable(char),
    56→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    57→      });
    58→    }
    59→
    60→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    61→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    62→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    63→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    64→    }
    65→
    66→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    67→      // Defensive release: if interactTarget is set but the character is no longer
    68→      // interacting, an external change (e.g. a stale async AI decision resolving
    69→      // between frames) moved them out of 'interacting' without triggering the
    70→      // normal detection below.  Release the slot now so the object doesn't stay
    71→      // permanently full.
    72→      if (char.interactTarget && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    73→        console.warn(
    74→          `[Engine] defensive release: ${char.name} has interactTarget ` +
    75→          `'${char.interactTarget}' but action='${char.action}' — releasing slot`
    76→        );
    77→        this.objectEngine.release(char.interactTarget, char.name);
    78→        char.interactTarget = null;
    79→      }
    80→
    81→      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions
    82→      const prevAction         = char.action;
    83→      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;
    84→
    85→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    86→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    87→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    88→      }
    89→
    90→      // Handle arrival: character reached talk target
    91→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    92→        this._handleTalkArrival(char);
    93→      }
    94→
    95→      // Mid-walk: periodically re-route toward a moving talk target
    96→      if (char.action === 'walking' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    97→        char._talkRetargetTimer -= deltaMs;
    98→        if (char._talkRetargetTimer <= 0) {
    99→          char._talkRetargetTimer = 2000; // re-check every 2 s
   100→          this._updateTalkRoute(char);
   101→        }
   102→      }
   103→
   104→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
   105→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
   106→        this._doWander(char);
   107→      }
   108→
   109→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
   110→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
   111→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
   112→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
   113→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
   114→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
   115→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
   116→        }
   117→      }
   118→
   119→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
   120→      char.update(deltaMs);
   121→
   122→      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object
   123→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
   124→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
   125→      }
   126→    }
   127→  }
   128→
   129→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   130→
   131→  /**
   132→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   133→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   134→   * If the object has no valid transition, finds an alternative instead of idling.
   135→   */
   136→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   137→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   138→    const action   = char.pendingAction || 'use';
   139→
   140→    // Clear targeting immediately so we don't re-fire on the next idle frame.
   141→    // _fallbackToAlternativeObject may set a new targetObjectId if it finds one.
   142→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   143→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   144→
   145→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   146→
   147→    if (event) {
   148→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   149→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   150→
   151→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   152→
   153→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   154→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   155→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   156→      if (obj && event.state) {
   157→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   158→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   159→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   160→        }
   161→      }
   162→
   163→      // Face toward the object tile before entering interaction
   164→      if (obj) {
   165→        const dx = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   166→        const dy = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   167→        if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   168→          char.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   169→        } else {
   170→          char.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   171→        }
   172→      }
   173→
   174→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs, obj?.interactAnim ?? null);
   175→
   176→      if (event.speech) char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   177→      if (event.emoji)  this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   178→    } else {
   179→      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) — release the
   180→      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.
   181→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   182→      this._fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, objectId);
   183→    }
   184→  }
   185→
   186→  // ── Talk handshake ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   187→
   188→  /**
   189→   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.
   190→   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.
   191→   */
   192→  _handleTalkArrival(char) {
   193→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   194→    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;
   195→
   196→    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.
   197→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   198→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   199→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   200→
   201→    if (dist > 3) {
   202→      // Target has drifted — try to follow if not too far
   203→      if (dist <= 10) {
   204→        const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);
   205→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty), dynWalkable);
   206→        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty, dynWalkable)) {
   207→          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival
   208→          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   209→          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;
   210→          return;
   211→        }
   212→      }
   213→      // Too far or unreachable — abort
   214→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   215→        type:      'fallback',
   216→        charLabel: char.label,
   217→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   218→        fromLabel: target.label,
   219→        toLabel:   null,
   220→      });
   221→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   222→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   223→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   224→      return;
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy
   228→    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   229→
   230→    if (!canTalk) {
   231→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   232→        type:           'talk_rejected',
   233→        initiatorLabel: char.label,
   234→        targetLabel:    target.label,
   235→      });
   236→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   237→      return;
   238→    }
   239→
   240→    this._startConversation(char, target);
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  /**
   244→   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).
   245→   * Defaults to 10–15 s; override via constructor config.
   246→   */
   247→  get _talkDurationMs() {
   248→    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;
   249→  }
   250→
   251→  /**
   252→   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.
   253→   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),
   254→   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.
   255→   */
   256→  _startConversation(charA, charB) {
   257→    // Release any pending object reservation charB held while walking.
   258→    // startTalk() clears targetObjectId without calling objectEngine.release(),
   259→    // so we must do it here before the slot becomes permanently orphaned.
   260→    if (charB.targetObjectId) {
   261→      this.objectEngine.release(charB.targetObjectId, charB.name);
   262→      charB.targetObjectId = null;
   263→      charB.pendingAction  = null;
   264→    }
   265→
   266→    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;
   267→
   268→    // Face each other
   269→    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);
   270→    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);
   271→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   272→      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   273→      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';
   274→    } else {
   275→      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   276→      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';
   277→    }
   278→
   279→    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles
   280→    if (charA.pendingTalkDialogue) {
   281→      charA.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkDialogue;
   282→      charA.pendingTalkDialogue    = null;
   283→    }
   284→    if (charA.pendingTalkResponse) {
   285→      charB.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkResponse;
   286→      charA.pendingTalkResponse    = null;
   287→    }
   288→
   289→    charA.startTalk(charB, duration);
   290→    charB.startTalk(charA, duration);
   291→
   292→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   293→      type:           'conversation_start',
   294→      initiatorLabel: charA.label,
   295→      targetLabel:    charB.label,
   296→    });
   297→  }
   298→
   299→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   300→
   301→  _doWander(char) {
   302→    // Build a walkable grid that treats other characters' tiles as obstacles
   303→    const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);
   304→
   305→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   306→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   307→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   308→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   309→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   310→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   311→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   312→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   313→          // Only target objects whose current state accepts a 'use' interaction
   314→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   315→          if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   316→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty, dynWalkable);
   317→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty, dynWalkable)) {
   318→            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking
   319→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   320→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   321→            return;
   322→          }
   323→        }
   324→        // All objects full/non-interactable/unreachable — fall through to random wander
   325→      }
   326→    }
   327→
   328→    // Random walkable tile
   329→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   330→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   331→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   332→      return;
   333→    }
   334→
   335→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   336→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   337→
   338→    let moved = false;
   339→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   340→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   341→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   342→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty, dynWalkable);
   343→      if (moved) break;
   344→    }
   345→
   346→    if (!moved) {
   347→      char._failedMoveCount++;
   348→      if (char._failedMoveCount >= 3) {
   349→        // Deadlock escape: step onto any free adjacent tile to break the standstill
   350→        char._failedMoveCount = 0;
   351→        const escapeTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(cx, cy, dynWalkable);
   352→        if (escapeTile) char.moveTo(escapeTile.tx, escapeTile.ty, dynWalkable);
   353→      }
   354→      // Retry quickly — the blocking character will likely have moved by then
   355→      char.wanderTimer = 500 + Math.random() * 500;
   356→    }
   357→  }
   358→
   359→  // ── Fallback helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   360→
   361→  /**
   362→   * Find the closest available object that `char` can interact with right now,
   363→   * excluding the object with `excludeId`.
   364→   * @returns {ObjectInstance|null}
   365→   */
   366→  _findAlternativeObject(char, excludeId) {
   367→    const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   368→    let best     = null;
   369→    let bestDist = Infinity;
   370→
   371→    for (const obj of objects) {
   372→      if (obj.id === excludeId) continue;
   373→      if (obj.isFull()) continue;
   374→      // Require a usable state right now
   375→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   376→      if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   377→      // Require a reachable adjacent tile
   378→      if (!this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty)) continue;
   379→
   380→      const dx   = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   381→      const dy   = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   382→      const dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
   383→      if (dist < bestDist) { bestDist = dist; best = obj; }
   384→    }
   385→
   386→    return best;
   387→  }
   388→
   389→  /**
   390→   * Called when a character's object interaction fails on arrival.
   391→   * Tries to redirect to the nearest available alternative; emits a 'fallback' event.
   392→   */
   393→  _fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, fromId) {
   394→    const fromObj     = this.objectEngine.getById(fromId);
   395→    const alternative = this._findAlternativeObject(char, fromId);
   396→
   397→    if (alternative) {
   398→      const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);
   399→      const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(alternative.tx, alternative.ty, dynWalkable);
   400→      if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty, dynWalkable)) {
   401→        alternative.reserve(char.name);
   402→        char.targetObjectId = alternative.id;
   403→        char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   404→
   405→        this.pendingEvents.push({
   406→          type:      'fallback',
   407→          charLabel: char.label,
   408→          reason:    'object_unavailable',
   409→          fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   410→          toLabel:   alternative.name,
   411→        });
   412→        return;
   413→      }
   414→    }
   415→
   416→    // No usable alternative — idle
   417→    char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   418→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   419→      type:      'fallback',
   420→      charLabel: char.label,
   421→      reason:    'object_unavailable',
   422→      fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   423→      toLabel:   null,
   424→    });
   425→  }
   426→
   427→  /**
   428→   * Called periodically while a character is walking toward a talk target.
   429→   * Re-routes the character if the target has moved, or aborts if too far.
   430→   */
   431→  _updateTalkRoute(char) {
   432→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   433→    if (!target) return;
   434→
   435→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   436→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   437→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   438→
   439→    // If target has wandered more than 10 tiles away, give up
   440→    if (dist > 10) {
   441→      char.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   442→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   443→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   444→      char.path                = [];
   445→      char.action              = 'idle';
   446→      char.wanderTimer         = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   447→
   448→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   449→        type:      'fallback',
   450→        charLabel: char.label,
   451→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   452→        fromLabel: target.label,
   453→        toLabel:   null,
   454→      });
   455→      return;
   456→    }
   457→
   458→    // Re-route only if the path end has drifted more than 1 tile from target
   459→    const pathEnd = char.path[char.path.length - 1];
   460→    if (pathEnd) {
   461→      const edx = pathEnd.tx - Math.round(target.tx);
   462→      const edy = pathEnd.ty - Math.round(target.ty);
   463→      if (Math.sqrt(edx * edx + edy * edy) > 1) {
   464→        const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);
   465→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty), dynWalkable);
   466→        if (adjTile) char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty, dynWalkable);
   467→      }
   468→    }
   469→  }
   470→
   471→  /**
   472→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   473→   * @param {boolean[][]} [walkable] - grid to check; defaults to the static this.walkable
   474→   */
   475→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty, walkable = this.walkable) {
   476→    const dirs = [
   477→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   478→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   479→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   480→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   481→    ];
   482→    for (const d of dirs) {
   483→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   484→        if (walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   485→      }
   486→    }
   487→    return null;
   488→  }
   489→
   490→  /**
   491→   * Clone the static walkable grid and mark every other character's current tile
   492→   * as blocked.  The calling character's own tile is left walkable.
   493→   * @param {object} excludeChar - the character doing the pathfinding (not blocked)
   494→   * @returns {boolean[][]}
   495→   */
   496→  _buildDynamicWalkable(excludeChar) {
   497→    const dynamic = this.walkable.map(row => row.slice());
   498→    for (const char of this.characters) {
   499→      if (char === excludeChar) continue;
   500→      const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   501→      const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   502→      if (cy >= 0 && cy < this.gridRows && cx >= 0 && cx < this.gridCols) {
   503→        dynamic[cy][cx] = false;
   504→      }
   505→    }
   506→    return dynamic;
   507→  }
   508→
   509→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   510→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   511→    const tiles = [];
   512→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   513→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   514→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   515→      }
   516→    }
   517→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   518→    return tiles;
   519→  }
   520→
   521→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   522→
   523→  getSimTimeString() {
   524→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   525→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   526→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   527→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   528→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   529→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   530→  }
   531→}
   532→

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    45\u2192\n    46\u2192  update(deltaMs) {\n    47\u2192    // Advance sim clock\n    48\u2192    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;\n    49\u2192\n    50\u2192    // Optional AI decisions \u2014 pass live object list so AI sees current states\n    51\u2192    if (this.aiEngine) {\n    52\u2192      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {\n    53\u2192        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),\n    54\u2192        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),\n    55\u2192        buildDynamicWalkable: (char) => this._buildDynamicWalkable(char),\n    56\u2192        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),\n    57\u2192      });\n    58\u2192    }\n    59\u2192\n    60\u2192    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events\n    61\u2192    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);\n    62\u2192    for (const ev of objEvents) {\n    63\u2192      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);\n    64\u2192    }\n    65\u2192\n    66\u2192    for (const char of this.characters) {\n    67\u2192      // Defensive release: if interactTarget is set but the character is no longer\n    68\u2192      // interacting, an external change (e.g. a stale async AI decision resolving\n    69\u2192      // between frames) moved them out of 'interacting' without triggering the\n    70\u2192      // normal detection below.  Release the slot now so the object doesn't stay\n    71\u2192      // permanently full.\n    72\u2192      if (char.interactTarget && char.action !== 'interacting') {\n    73\u2192 slot`\n    76\u2192        );\n    77\u2192        this.objectEngine.release(char.interactTarget, char.name);\n    78\u2192        char.interactTarget = null;\n    79\u2192      }\n    80\u2192\n    81\u2192      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions\n    82\u2192      const prevAction         = char.action;\n    83\u2192      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;\n    84\u2192\n    85\u2192      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile\n    86\u2192      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {\n    87\u2192        this._handleObjectArrival(char);\n    88\u2192      }\n    89\u2192\n    90\u2192      // Handle arrival: character reached talk target\n    91\u2192      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {\n    92\u2192        this._handleTalkArrival(char);\n    93\u2192      }\n    94\u2192\n    95\u2192      // Mid-walk: periodically re-route toward a moving talk target\n    96\u2192      if (char.action === 'walking' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {\n    97\u2192        char._talkRetargetTimer -= deltaMs;\n    98\u2192        if (char._talkRetargetTimer <= 0) {\n    99\u2192          char._talkRetargetTimer = 2000; // re-check every 2 s\n   100\u2192          this._updateTalkRoute(char);\n   101\u2192        }\n   102\u2192      }\n   103\u2192\n   104\u2192      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired\n   105\u2192      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {\n   106\u2192        this._doWander(char);\n   107\u2192      }\n   108\u2192\n   109\u2192      // Tick speech timer \u2014 fire a random line when it expires\n   110\u2192      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {\n   111\u2192        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;\n   112\u2192        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {\n   113\u2192          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);\n   114\u2192          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];\n   115\u2192          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20\u201340 s\n   116\u2192        }\n   117\u2192      }\n   118\u2192\n   119\u2192      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)\n   120\u2192      char.update(deltaMs);\n   121\u2192\n   122\u2192      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object\n   123\u2192      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {\n   124\u2192        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);\n   125\u2192      }\n   126\u2192    }\n   127\u2192  }\n   128\u2192\n   129\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Object interaction \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n   130\u2192\n   131\u2192  /**\n   132\u2192   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.\n   133\u2192   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.\n   134\u2192   * If the object has no valid transition, finds an alternative instead of idling.\n   135\u2192   */\n   136\u2192  _handleObjectArrival(char) {\n   137\u2192    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;\n   138\u2192    const action   = char.pendingAction || 'use';\n   139\u2192\n   140\u2192    // Clear targeting immediately so we don't re-fire on the next idle frame.\n   141\u2192    // _fallbackToAlternativeObject may set a new targetObjectId if it finds one.\n   142\u2192    char.targetObjectId = null;\n   143\u2192    char.pendingAction  = null;\n   144\u2192\n   145\u2192    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);\n   146\u2192\n   147\u2192    if (event) {\n   148\u2192      // Convert reservation \u2192 active occupancy\n   149\u2192 auto_next duration if the new state has one;\n   154\u2192      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.\n   155\u2192      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;\n   156\u2192      if (obj && event.state) {\n   157\u2192        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];\n   158\u2192        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {\n   159\u2192          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;\n   160\u2192        }\n   161\u2192      }\n   162\u2192\n   163\u2192      // Face toward the object tile before entering interaction\n   164\u2192      if (obj) {\n   165\u2192        const dx = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);\n   166\u2192        const dy = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);\n   167\u2192        if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {\n   168\u2192          char.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';\n   169\u2192        } else {\n   170\u2192          char.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';\n   171\u2192        }\n   172\u2192      }\n   173\u2192\n   174\u2192      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs, obj?.interactAnim ?? null);\n   175\u2192\n   176\u2192      if (event.speech) char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;\n   177\u2192      if (event.emoji)  this.pendingEvents.push(event);\n   178\u2192    } else {\n   179\u2192      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) \u2014 release the\n   180\u2192      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.\n   181\u2192      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);\n   182\u2192 \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n   187\u2192\n   188\u2192  /**\n   189\u2192   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.\n   190\u2192   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.\n   191\u2192   */\n   192\u2192  _handleTalkArrival(char) {\n   193\u2192    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;\n   194\u2192    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;\n   195\u2192\n   196\u2192    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.\n   197\u2192    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);\n   198\u2192    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);\n   199\u2192    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n   200\u2192\n   201\u2192    if (dist > 3) {\n   202\u2192      // Target has drifted \u2014 try to follow if not too far\n   203\u2192      if (dist <= 10) {\n   204\u2192        const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);\n   205\u2192        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty), dynWalkable);\n   206\u2192        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty, dynWalkable)) {\n   207\u2192          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival\n   208\u2192          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;\n   209\u2192          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;\n   210\u2192          return;\n   211\u2192        }\n   212\u2192      }\n   213\u2192      // Too far or unreachable \u2014 abort\n   214\u2192      this.pendingEvents.push({\n   215\u2192        type:      'fallback',\n   216\u2192        charLabel: char.label,\n   217\u2192        reason:    'talk_target_moved',\n   218\u2192        fromLabel: target.label,\n   219\u2192        toLabel:   null,\n   220\u2192      });\n   221\u2192      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;\n   222\u2192      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;\n   223\u2192      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;\n   224\u2192      return;\n   225\u2192    }\n   226\u2192\n   227\u2192    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy\n   228\u2192    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';\n   229\u2192\n   230\u2192    if (!canTalk) {\n   231\u2192      this.pendingEvents.push({\n   232\u2192        type:           'talk_rejected',\n   233\u2192        initiatorLabel: char.label,\n   234\u2192        targetLabel:    target.label,\n   235\u2192      });\n   236\u2192      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;\n   237\u2192      return;\n   238\u2192    }\n   239\u2192\n   240\u2192    this._startConversation(char, target);\n   241\u2192  }\n   242\u2192\n   243\u2192  /**\n   244\u2192   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).\n   245\u2192   * Defaults to 10\u201315 s; override via constructor config.\n   246\u2192   */\n   247\u2192  get _talkDurationMs() {\n   248\u2192    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;\n   249\u2192  }\n   250\u2192\n   251\u2192  /**\n   252\u2192   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.\n   253\u2192   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),\n   254\u2192   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.\n   255\u2192   */\n   256\u2192  _startConversation(charA, charB) {\n   257\u2192    // Release any pending object reservation charB held while walking.\n   258\u2192    // startTalk() clears targetObjectId without calling objectEngine.release(),\n   259\u2192    // so we must do it here before the slot becomes permanently orphaned.\n   260\u2192    if (charB.targetObjectId) {\n   261\u2192      this.objectEngine.release(charB.targetObjectId, charB.name);\n   262\u2192      charB.targetObjectId = null;\n   263\u2192      charB.pendingAction  = null;\n   264\u2192    }\n   265\u2192\n   266\u2192    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;\n   267\u2192\n   268\u2192    // Face each other\n   269\u2192    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);\n   270\u2192    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);\n   271\u2192    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {\n   272\u2192      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';\n   273\u2192      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';\n   274\u2192    } else {\n   275\u2192      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';\n   276\u2192      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';\n   277\u2192    }\n   278\u2192\n   279\u2192    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles\n   280\u2192    if (charA.pendingTalkDialogue) {\n   281\u2192      charA.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkDialogue;\n   282\u2192      charA.pendingTalkDialogue    = null;\n   283\u2192    }\n   284\u2192    if (charA.pendingTalkResponse) {\n   285\u2192      charB.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkResponse;\n   286\u2192      charA.pendingTalkResponse    = null;\n   287\u2192    }\n   288\u2192\n   289\u2192    charA.startTalk(charB, duration);\n   290\u2192    charB.startTalk(charA, duration);\n   291\u2192\n   292\u2192    this.pendingEvents.push({\n   293\u2192      type:           'conversation_start',\n   294\u2192      initiatorLabel: charA.label,\n   295\u2192      targetLabel:    charB.label,\n   296\u2192    });\n   297\u2192  }\n   298\u2192\n   299\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Wander \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n   300\u2192\n   301\u2192  _doWander(char) {\n   302\u2192    // Build a walkable grid that treats other characters' tiles as obstacles\n   303\u2192    const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);\n   304\u2192\n   305\u2192    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely\n   306\u2192    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {\n   307\u2192      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();\n   308\u2192      if (objects.length > 0) {\n   309\u2192        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile\n   310\u2192        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\n   311\u2192        for (const obj of shuffled) {\n   312\u2192          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity\n   313\u2192          // Only target objects whose current state accepts a 'use' interaction\n   314\u2192          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n   315\u2192          if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;\n   316\u2192          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty, dynWalkable);\n   317\u2192          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty, dynWalkable)) {\n   318\u2192            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking\n   319\u2192            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;\n   320\u2192            char.pendingAction  = 'use';\n   321\u2192            return;\n   322\u2192          }\n   323\u2192        }\n   324\u2192        // All objects full/non-interactable/unreachable \u2014 fall through to random wander\n   325\u2192      }\n   326\u2192    }\n   327\u2192\n   328\u2192    // Random walkable tile\n   329\u2192    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();\n   330\u2192    if (tiles.length === 0) {\n   331\u2192      char.wanderTimer = 2000;\n   332\u2192      return;\n   333\u2192    }\n   334\u2192\n   335\u2192    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);\n   336\u2192    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);\n   337\u2192\n   338\u2192    let moved = false;\n   339\u2192    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {\n   340\u2192      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];\n   341\u2192      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;\n   342\u2192      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty, dynWalkable);\n   343\u2192      if (moved) break;\n   344\u2192    }\n   345\u2192\n   346\u2192    if (!moved) {\n   347\u2192      char._failedMoveCount++;\n   348\u2192      if (char._failedMoveCount >= 3) {\n   349\u2192        // Deadlock escape: step onto any free adjacent tile to break the standstill\n   350\u2192        char._failedMoveCount = 0;\n   351\u2192        const escapeTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(cx, cy, dynWalkable);\n   352\u2192        if (escapeTile) char.moveTo(escapeTile.tx, escapeTile.ty, dynWalkable);\n   353\u2192      }\n   354\u2192      // Retry quickly \u2014 the blocking character will likely have moved by then\n   355\u2192      char.wanderTimer = 500 + Math.random() * 500;\n   356\u2192    }\n   357\u2192  }\n   358\u2192\n   359\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Fallback helpers \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n   360\u2192\n   361\u2192  /**\n   362\u2192   * Find the closest available object that `char` can interact with right now,\n   363\u2192   * excluding the object with `excludeId`.\n   364\u2192   * @returns {ObjectInstance|null}\n   365\u2192   */\n   366\u2192  _findAlternativeObject(char, excludeId) {\n   367\u2192    const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();\n   368\u2192    let best     = null;\n   369\u2192    let bestDist = Infinity;\n   370\u2192\n   371\u2192    for (const obj of objects) {\n   372\u2192      if (obj.id === excludeId) continue;\n   373\u2192      if (obj.isFull()) 381\u2192      const dy   = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);\n   382\u2192      const dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;\n   383\u2192      if (dist < bestDist) { bestDist = dist; best = obj; }\n   384\u2192    }\n   385\u2192\n   386\u2192    return best;\n   387\u2192  }\n   388\u2192\n   389\u2192  /**\n   390\u2192   * Called when a character's object interaction fails on arrival.\n   391\u2192   * Tries to redirect to the nearest available alternative; emits a 'fallback' event.\n   392\u2192   */\n   393\u2192  _fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, fromId) {\n   394\u2192    const fromObj     = this.objectEngine.getById(fromId);\n   395\u2192    const alternative = this._findAlternativeObject(char, fromId);\n   396\u2192\n   397\u2192    if (alternative) {\n   398\u2192      const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);\n   399\u2192      const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(alternative.tx, alternative.ty, dynWalkable);\n   400\u2192      if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty, dynWalkable)) {\n   401\u2192        alternative.reserve(char.name);\n   402\u2192        char.targetObjectId = alternative.id;\n   403\u2192        char.pendingAction  = 'use';\n   404\u2192\n   405\u2192        this.pendingEvents.push({\n   406\u2192          type:      'fallback',\n   407\u2192          charLabel: char.label,\n   408\u2192          reason:    'object_unavailable',\n   409\u2192          fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,\n   410\u2192          toLabel:   alternative.name,\n   411\u2192        });\n   412\u2192        return;\n   413\u2192      }\n   414\u2192    }\n   415\u2192\n   416\u2192    // No usable alternative \u2014 idle\n   417\u2192    char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;\n   418\u2192    this.pendingEvents.push({\n   419\u2192      type:      'fallback',\n   420\u2192      charLabel: char.label,\n   421\u2192      reason:    'object_unavailable',\n   422\u2192      fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,\n   423\u2192      toLabel:   null,\n   424\u2192    });\n   425\u2192  }\n   426\u2192\n   427\u2192  /**\n   428\u2192   * Called periodically while a character is walking toward a talk target.\n   429\u2192   * Re-routes the character if the target has moved, or aborts if too far.\n   430\u2192   */\n   431\u2192  _updateTalkRoute(char) {\n   432\u2192    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;\n   433\u2192    if (!target) return;\n   434\u2192\n   435\u2192    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);\n   436\u2192    const dy   = 440\u2192    if (dist > 10) {\n   441\u2192      char.pendingTalkTarget   = null;\n   442\u2192      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;\n   443\u2192      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;\n   444\u2192 The stove stays as stove_off.png even when its state is cooking or done. Books stay closed. Easel stays blank. Object state machines work internally but have no visual feedback.

## Available Assets

* stove_off.png / stove_on.png
* book_closed.png / book_open.png
* easel_blank.png / easel_painting.png / easel_finished.png

     1→import { Character }         from './Character.js';
     2→import { SimulationEngine } from './Engine.js';
     3→import { AIEngine }          from './AIEngine.js';
     4→import { showSpeech }        from './speechBubble.js';
     5→import { OBJECT_DEFS }       from './objects.js';
     6→
     7→// ─── Constants ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     8→
     9→const TILE_SIZE  = 48;
    10→const GRID_COLS  = 19;
    11→const GRID_ROWS  = 13;
    12→
    13→// Walk spritesheet layout (2304×864, 48 cols × 9 rows, frame size 48×96)
    14→// Frame number = row * 48 + col.  Verified by visual inspection:
    15→//   Row 0 → up   (4 frames:  0–3)
    16→//   Row 3 → right (6 frames: 144–149)
    17→//   Row 6 → down  (6 frames: 288–293)
    18→// LEFT reuses the RIGHT frames with flipX applied at runtime.
    19→const WALK_DIRS = [
    20→  { key: 'up',    start:   0, end:   3 },
    21→  { key: 'down',  start: 288, end: 293 },
    22→  { key: 'right', start: 144, end: 149 },
    23→  { key: 'left',  start: 144, end: 149 }, // mirrored via flipX
    24→];
    25→
    26→// Character definitions — tile positions within walkable area (col 1–17, row 2–9)
    27→const CHARS = [
    28→  {
    29→    name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6, ty: 7,
    30→    dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?', 'The kitchen smells amazing'],
    31→  },
    32→  {
    33→    name: 'Lucy', label: 'Sol', tx: 10, ty: 6,
    34→    dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'I should water the plants', 'Such peaceful light...'],
    35→  },
    36→  {
    37→    name: 'Ash', label: 'Nyx', tx: 13, ty: 5,
    38→    dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect for sketching', 'Where did I put my brush?'],
    39→  },
    40→];
    41→
    42→// ─── Walkable grid ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    43→// 19 cols × 13 rows.
    44→// Interior floor (main room): cols 1–17, rows 2–9.
    45→// Rows 0–1 = roof/top wall; rows 10–12 = genkan / exterior — not walkable.
    46→
    47→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    48→  const grid = [];
    49→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    50→    const r = [];
    51→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    52→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    53→    }
    54→    grid.push(r);
    55→  }
    56→  // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
    57→  for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
    58→    const { tx, ty } = def.position;
    59→    if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}
    65→
    66→// ─── Scene ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    67→
    68→export class CafeScene extends Phaser.Scene {
    69→  constructor() { super({ key: 'CafeScene' }); }
    70→
    71→  // ── Preload ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    72→
    73→  preload() {
    74→    this.load.image('jp', 'assets/designs/Japanese_Home_1_preview_48x48.png');
    75→
    76→    // Object state sprites (one image per visual state)
    77→    [
    78→      'stove_off', 'stove_on',
    79→      'book_closed', 'book_open',
    80→      'easel_blank', 'easel_painting', 'easel_finished',
    81→      'cup_empty', 'cup_full',
    82→    ].forEach(key => this.load.image(key, `assets/sprites/${key}.png`));
    83→
    84→    // Interaction animation types → spritesheets (48×96 frames, 6 frames each)
    85→    const INTERACT_ANIMS = ['reading_48x48', 'sit_48x48', 'sit2_48x48', 'phone_48x48'];
    86→
    87→    ['Amelia', 'Lucy', 'Ash'].forEach(name => {
    88→      this.load.spritesheet(`${name}_idle`, `assets/characters/${name}_idle.png`, {
    89→        frameWidth: 48, frameHeight: 96,
    90→      });
    91→      this.load.spritesheet(`${name}_walk`, `assets/characters/${name}_walk.png`, {
    92→        frameWidth: 48, frameHeight: 96,
    93→      });
    94→      INTERACT_ANIMS.forEach(anim => {
    95→        this.load.spritesheet(`${name}_${anim}`, `assets/characters/${name}_${anim}.png`, {
    96→          frameWidth: 48, frameHeight: 96,
    97→        });
    98→      });
    99→    });
   100→  }
   101→
   102→  // ── Create ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   103→
   104→  create() {
   105→    // Background
   106→    const img = this.add.image(0, 0, 'jp').setOrigin(0, 0);
   107→    this.cameras.main.setBounds(0, 0, img.width, img.height);
   108→    this.cameras.main.centerOn(img.width / 2, img.height / 2);
   109→
   110→    // Object state sprites — overlaid on the background tile, swapped on state transitions
   111→    // Objects with spriteMap: stove, tea_set, bookshelf, easel
   112→    this._objectSprites = {};
   113→    for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   114→      if (!def.spriteMap) continue;
   115→      const initKey = def.spriteMap[def.state] ?? null;
   116→      if (!initKey) continue;
   117→      const px = def.position.tx * TILE_SIZE;
   118→      const py = def.position.ty * TILE_SIZE;
   119→      this._objectSprites[def.id] = this.add.image(px, py, initKey)
   120→        .setOrigin(0, 0)
   121→        .setDepth(1);
   122→    }
   123→
   124→    // Interaction animation type → Phaser anim key suffix and spritesheet key suffix
   125→    const INTERACT_ANIM_DEFS = [
   126→      { type: 'reading', sheetKey: 'reading_48x48' },
   127→      { type: 'sit',     sheetKey: 'sit_48x48'     },
   128→      { type: 'sit2',    sheetKey: 'sit2_48x48'    },
   129→      { type: 'phone',   sheetKey: 'phone_48x48'   },
   130→    ];
   131→
   132→    // Animations
   133→    ['Amelia', 'Lucy', 'Ash'].forEach(name => {
   134→      this.anims.create({
   135→        key: `${name}_idle_anim`,
   136→        frames: this.anims.generateFrameNumbers(`${name}_idle`, { start: 0, end: 5 }),
   137→        frameRate: 6,
   138→        repeat: -1,
   139→      });
   140→
   141→      WALK_DIRS.forEach(({ key, start, end }) => {
   142→        this.anims.create({
   143→          key: `${name}_walk_${key}`,
   144→          frames: this.anims.generateFrameNumbers(`${name}_walk`, { start, end }),
   145→          frameRate: 8,
   146→          repeat: -1,
   147→        });
   148→      });
   149→
   150→      // Interaction animations (6-frame loop, 6 fps)
   151→      INTERACT_ANIM_DEFS.forEach(({ type, sheetKey }) => {
   152→        this.anims.create({
   153→          key: `${name}_interact_${type}`,
   154→          frames: this.anims.generateFrameNumbers(`${name}_${sheetKey}`, { start: 0, end: 5 }),
   155→          frameRate: 6,
   156→          repeat: -1,
   157→        });
   158→      });
   159→    });
   160→
   161→    // Engine
   162→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   163→    this.engine = new SimulationEngine({

   165→      gridCols: GRID_COLS,
   166→      gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   167→      aiEngine: new AIEngine({
   168→        endpoint: '/api/llm',
   169→        model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   170→        decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,
   171→      }),
   172→    });
   173→
   174→    // Characters
   175→    CHARS.forEach(({ name, label, tx, ty, dialogue }) => {
   176→      const initPx = tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   177→      const initPy = (ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   178→
   179→      const sprite = this.add.sprite(initPx, initPy, `${name}_idle`)
   180→        .setOrigin(0.5, 1)
   181→        .setDepth(10);
   182→      sprite.play(`${name}_idle_anim`);
   183→
   184→      const nameLabel = this.add.text(initPx, initPy - 100, label, {
   185→        fontSize: '12px',
   186→        color: '#ffffff',
   187→        fontFamily: 'monospace',
   188→        stroke: '#000000',
   189→        strokeThickness: 2,
   190→      }).setOrigin(0.5, 1).setDepth(11);
   191→
   192→      const char = new Character({
   193→        name, label, tx, ty, sprite, nameLabel,
   194→        walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   195→        dialogue,
   196→      });
   197→
   198→      this.engine.addCharacter(char);
   199→    });
   200→
   201→    // Expose engine for the debug overlay panel
   202→    window._gameEngine = this.engine;
   203→
   204→    // Sim clock display (screen-fixed, top-left)
   205→    this.clockText = this.add.text(8, 8, '', {
   206→      fontSize: '13px',
   207→      color: '#ffe8a3',
   208→      fontFamily: 'monospace',
   209→      stroke: '#000000',
   210→      strokeThickness: 2,
   211→    }).setDepth(20).setScrollFactor(0);
   212→  }
   213→
   214→  // ── Update ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   215→
   216→  update(_time, delta) {
   217→    this.engine.update(delta);
   218→    this.clockText.setText(this.engine.getSimTimeString());
   219→
   220→    // Show speech bubbles queued by the engine
   221→    for (const char of this.engine.characters) {
   222→      if (char.pendingSpeech && char.sprite) {
   223→        showSpeech(this, char.sprite, char.pendingSpeech);
   224→        char.pendingSpeech = null;
   225→      }
   226→    }
   227→
   228→    // Process object state-transition events: swap sprites and float emojis
   229→    if (this.engine.pendingEvents.length > 0) {
   230→      for (const ev of this.engine.pendingEvents) {
   231→        const obj = this.engine.objectEngine.getById(ev.objectId);
   232→        if (!obj) continue;
   233→
   234→        // Swap object sprite texture on state change
   235→        if (ev.spriteKey && this._objectSprites[ev.objectId]) {
   236→          this._objectSprites[ev.objectId].setTexture(ev.spriteKey);
   237→        }
   238→
   239→        // Float emoji above the object
   240→        if (ev.emoji) {
   241→          const px = obj.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   242→          const py = obj.ty * TILE_SIZE;

   244→          this.tweens.add({
   245→            targets: label,
   246→            y:       label.y - 40,
   247→            alpha:   0,
   248→            duration: 2000,
   249→            onComplete: () => label.destroy(),
   250→          });
   251→        }
   252→      }
   253→      this.engine.pendingEvents = [];
   254→    }
   255→  }

{"id":"FRG-246","title":"Objects change sprite when state transitions","description":"## Problem

The stove stays as stove_off.png even when its state is cooking or done. Books stay closed. Easel stays blank. Object state machines work internally but have no visual feedback.

## Available Assets

* stove_off.png / stove_on.png
* book_closed.png / book_open.png
* easel_blank.png / easel_painting.png / easel_finished.png
* cup_empty.png / cup_full.png

## What to do

1. Define a sprite map per object: { stateName: spriteKey }
2. On each state transition (in objectEngine), emit the new sprite key
3. Scene.js swaps the sprite texture on the Phaser game object
4. Map: stove cooking/done->stove_on, idle->stove_off; bookshelf reading->book_open, idle->book_closed; easel painting->easel_painting, done->easel_finished, idle->easel_blank; tea_set brewing/ready->cup_full, idle->cup_empty

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #97
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/objects.js` — Added `spriteMap: { stateName: spriteKey }` to stove, tea_set, bookshelf, and easel defs; stored `spriteMap` on `ObjectInstance`; included `spriteKey` in events returned by `interact()` and `tick()` - `src/Engine.js` — Changed both event-push conditions to `ev.emoji || ev.spriteKey` so sprite-only transitions (no emoji) still reach the scene - `src/scene.js` — Preloads 9 object state sprites; overlays a `Phaser.GameObjects.Image` for each mapped object at its tile position; swaps texture via `setTexture(ev.spriteKey)` when a state-transition event arrives ## Key Decisions - Object sprites are placed at depth 1 (above background, below characters at depth 10) to avoid z-order issues - Used `setOrigin(0, 0)` to align sprites to the tile top-left, consistent with the background image placement - Sprite creation in `create()` iterates `OBJECT_DEFS` directly so any future object with a `spriteMap` gets a sprite automatically ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/FRG-246-object-sprite-state-transitions` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/18
